# Deployment Combination Search

Protocol: `full_history_deployment_discovery`.

This report is for choosing fixed combinations to deploy from completed historical rolling predictions. It intentionally uses all available historical prediction outcomes for model selection, so it is a deployment discovery leaderboard rather than a strict walk-forward model-selection validation.

Max pool size: `20`; pool sizes: `6,8,10,12,15,20`; rank metrics: `ba,auc,ap,brier`; scopes: `all`.
